Introduction

Base URL: http://0.0.0.0:8000 
This documentation aims to provide all the information you need to work with our API.

<aside>As you scroll, you'll see code examples for working with the API in different programming languages in the dark area to the right (or as part of the content on mobile).
You can switch the language used with the tabs at the top right (or from the nav menu at the top left on mobile).</aside>

Authenticating requests

This API is not authenticated.

Endpoints

POST api/authentication/login

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://0.0.0.0:8000/api/authentication/login" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"email\": \"gbailey@example.net\",
    \"password\": \"|]|{+-\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://0.0.0.0:8000/api/authentication/login"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "email": "gbailey@example.net",
    "password": "|]|{+-"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:


Tip: Check that you're properly connected to the network.
If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.
You can check the Dev Tools console for debugging information.

Request      

POST api/authentication/login

Headers

Content-Type        

Example: application/json

Accept        

Example: application/json

Body Parameters

email   string     

Must be a valid email address. Example: gbailey@example.net

password   string     

Example: |]|{+-

POST api/basic

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://0.0.0.0:8000/api/basic" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"name\": \"architecto\",
    \"label\": \"architecto\",
    \"email\": \"zbailey@example.net\",
    \"phone\": \"architecto\",
    \"url\": \"http:\\/\\/bailey.com\\/\",
    \"summary\": \"architecto\",
    \"location\": {
        \"address\": \"architecto\",
        \"postalCode\": \"architecto\",
        \"city\": \"architecto\",
        \"countryCode\": \"architecto\",
        \"region\": \"architecto\"
    },
    \"profiles\": [
        {
            \"network\": \"architecto\",
            \"username\": \"architecto\",
            \"url\": \"http:\\/\\/bailey.com\\/\"
        }
    ]
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://0.0.0.0:8000/api/basic"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "name": "architecto",
    "label": "architecto",
    "email": "zbailey@example.net",
    "phone": "architecto",
    "url": "http:\/\/bailey.com\/",
    "summary": "architecto",
    "location": {
        "address": "architecto",
        "postalCode": "architecto",
        "city": "architecto",
        "countryCode": "architecto",
        "region": "architecto"
    },
    "profiles": [
        {
            "network": "architecto",
            "username": "architecto",
            "url": "http:\/\/bailey.com\/"
        }
    ]
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:

If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.

GET api/basic

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://0.0.0.0:8000/api/basic" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://0.0.0.0:8000/api/basic"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};


fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

PATCH api/basic/{basic_id}

Example request:
curl --request PATCH \
    "http://0.0.0.0:8000/api/basic/architecto" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"name\": \"architecto\",
    \"label\": \"architecto\",
    \"email\": \"zbailey@example.net\",
    \"phone\": \"architecto\",
    \"url\": \"http:\\/\\/bailey.com\\/\",
    \"summary\": \"architecto\",
    \"location\": {
        \"address\": \"architecto\",
        \"postalCode\": \"architecto\",
        \"city\": \"architecto\",
        \"countryCode\": \"architecto\",
        \"region\": \"architecto\"
    },
    \"profiles\": [
        {
            \"network\": \"architecto\",
            \"username\": \"architecto\",
            \"url\": \"http:\\/\\/bailey.com\\/\"
        }
    ]
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://0.0.0.0:8000/api/basic/architecto"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "name": "architecto",
    "label": "architecto",
    "email": "zbailey@example.net",
    "phone": "architecto",
    "url": "http:\/\/bailey.com\/",

        "address": "architecto",

        {
            "network": "architecto",

PATCH api/certificate/{certificate_id}

Example request:
curl --request PATCH \
    "http://0.0.0.0:8000/api/certificate/architecto" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"name\": \"architecto\",
    \"date\": \"2026-02-19T18:54:26\",
    \"issuer\": \"architecto\",
    \"url\": \"http:\\/\\/bailey.com\\/\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://0.0.0.0:8000/api/certificate/architecto"

    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"name\": \"architecto\",
    \"position\": \"architecto\",
    \"url\": \"http:\\/\\/bailey.com\\/\",
    \"startDate\": \"architecto\",
    \"endDate\": \"architecto\",
    \"summary\": \"architecto\",
    \"highlights\": [
        \"architecto\"
    ]
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://0.0.0.0:8000/api/work/architecto"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "name": "architecto",
    "position": "architecto",
    "url": "http:\/\/bailey.com\/",
    "startDate": "architecto",
    "endDate": "architecto",
    "summary": "architecto",
    "highlights": [
        "architecto"
    ]
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "PATCH",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
